WITH 

/* 

[NAME]

- HANA_Threads_Callstacks_2.00.060+

[DESCRIPTION]

- Thread call stack details

[SOURCE]

- SAP Note 1969700

[DETAILS AND RESTRICTIONS]

- HOST_SERVICE_THREAD_CALLSTACKS.SITE_ID available with SAP HANA 2.0 SPS 06
- All information retrieved from M_SERVICE_THREAD_CALLSTACKS / HOST_SERVICE_THREAD_CALLSTACKS, no (potentially inconsistent join) with M_SERVICE_THREADS
- NO_USE_HEX_PLAN hint required to avoid running into the following error:

  too many statement recompile requests: max recompile limit exceeded

[VALID FOR]

- Revisions:              >= 2.00.060

[SQL COMMAND VERSION]

- 2025/12/30:  1.0 (initial version)

[INVOLVED TABLES]

- HOST_SERVICE_THREAD_CALLSTACKS
- M_SERVICE_THREAD_CALLSTACKS

[INPUT PARAMETERS]

- BEGIN_TIME

  Begin time

  '2018/12/05 14:05:00' --> Set begin time to 5th of December 2018, 14:05
  'C'                   --> Set begin time to current time
  'C-S900'              --> Set begin time to current time minus 900 seconds
  'C-M15'               --> Set begin time to current time minus 15 minutes
  'C-H5'                --> Set begin time to current time minus 5 hours
  'C-D1'                --> Set begin time to current time minus 1 day
  'C-W4'                --> Set begin time to current time minus 4 weeks
  'E-S900'              --> Set begin time to end time minus 900 seconds
  'E-M15'               --> Set begin time to end time minus 15 minutes
  'E-H5'                --> Set begin time to end time minus 5 hours
  'E-D1'                --> Set begin time to end time minus 1 day
  'E-W4'                --> Set begin time to end time minus 4 weeks
  'MIN'                 --> Set begin time to minimum (1000/01/01 00:00:00)

- END_TIME

  End time

  '2018/12/08 14:05:00' --> Set end time to 8th of December 2018, 14:05
  'C'                   --> Set end time to current time
  'C-S900'              --> Set end time to current time minus 900 seconds
  'C-M15'               --> Set end time to current time minus 15 minutes
  'C-H5'                --> Set end time to current time minus 5 hours
  'C-D1'                --> Set end time to current time minus 1 day
  'C-W4'                --> Set end time to current time minus 4 weeks
  'B+S900'              --> Set end time to begin time plus 900 seconds
  'B+M15'               --> Set end time to begin time plus 15 minutes
  'B+H5'                --> Set end time to begin time plus 5 hours
  'B+D1'                --> Set end time to begin time plus 1 day
  'B+W4'                --> Set end time to begin time plus 4 weeks
  'MAX'                 --> Set end time to maximum (9999/12/31 23:59:59)

- TIMEZONE

  Used timezone (both for input and output parameters)

  'SERVER'       --> Display times in SAP HANA server time
  'UTC'          --> Display times in UTC time

- SITE_ID

  System replication site ID (may only work for DATA_SOURCE = 'HISTORY')

  -1                --> No restriction related to site ID
  1                 --> Site ID 1
  CURRENT_SITE_ID() --> Current primary site ID

- HOST

  Host name

  'saphana01'     --> Specic host saphana01
  'saphana%'      --> All hosts starting with saphana
  '%'             --> All hosts

- PORT

  Port number

  '30007'         --> Port 30007
  '%03'           --> All ports ending with '03'
  '%'             --> No restriction to ports

- THREAD_ID

  Thread identifier

  4567            --> Thread 4567
  -1              --> No thread identifier restriction

- COMPONENTS

  Components involved in call stack (concatenated in alphabetic order)

  - A:  Attribute engine
  - C:  Calculation engine
  - E:  ESX (Extended SQL Executor) engine 
  - F:  Federation
  - H:  HEX / HANA execution engine
  - J:  Join engine
  - L:  L language processing
  - Li: liveCache
  - M:  Memory management operations
  - N:  TrexNet network operations
  - O:  OLAP engine
  - Os: Operating system calls
  - P:  Planning engine
  - Q:  qo3 query optimizer
  - R:  ptime / row engine
  - S:  SQLScript
  - U:  HUP (HANA update) engine
  - X:  X2 executor

  'M'             --> Threads executing memory management operations
  'AH'            --> Threads involving attribute engine and HEX engine
  '%Os%'          --> Threads executing operating system calls
  '%'             --> No thread component restriction

- THREAD_TYPE

  Type of thread (e.g. 'SqlExecutor', 'JobWorker' or 'MergedogMonitor')

  'SqlExecutor'   --> Threads with type 'SqlExecutor'
  '%'             --> No thread type restriction

- THREAD_CONTEXT

  Main thread context (determined dynamically based on call stack)

  'OlapEngine (ReadPartsJob)' --> Thread context "OlapEngine (ReadPartsJob)"
  '%DataAccess%'              --> All threads with contexts including DataAccess
  '%'                         --> No restriction related to thread context

- THREAD_ACTIVITY

  Current thread activity (determined dynamically based on call stack)

  'DataStatistics (getColumnStats)' --> Threads being active with "DataStatistics (getColumnStats)" processing
  '%ResourceManager%'               --> Threads with activities related to ResourceManager
  '%'                               --> No restriction related to thread activity

- THREAD_STATE 

  State of thread (e.g. e.g. 'Running', 'Network Poll' or 'Semaphore Wait')

  'Running'       --> Threads with state 'Running'
  '%'             --> No thread state restriction

- CALLSTACK_PATTERN

  Callstack pattern

  '%comm::read%'  --> Only show thread all stacks containing comm:read
  '%'             --> No restriction related to call stack

- MAX_FRAME_LEVEL

  Maximum call stack frame level (smaller values can improve the performance)

  10              --> Only display the 10 deepest levels of each call stack
  -1              --> Display up to 48 levels of each call stack

- MAX_CALL_LEN

  Maximum length of call information in output (longer values are truncated)

  40              --> Limit length of call information to 40
  -1              --> No restriction related to call length

- ONLY_ACTIVE_THREADS

  Possibility to restrict output to active threads

  'X'             --> Only call stacks for active threads are shown
  ' '             --> No restriction in terms of call stacks

- IGNORE_OWN_THREADS

  Possibility to exclude threads related to own connection

  'X'             --> Only show threads not belonging to own connection
  ' '             --> Show all threads

- ONLY_INDEX_HANDLE_CALLSTACKS

  Possibility to filter for index handle related call stacks (index handle waiters are excluded)

  'X'             --> Display only call stacks that most likely have acquired an index handle
  ' '             --> No restriction related to index handle call stacks

- SHORT_CALLS

  Possibility to activate a reduced output of call information

  'X'             --> Display only the main procedure
  ' '             --> Display complete call information

- DATA_SOURCE

  Source of analysis data

  'CURRENT'       --> Data from memory information (M_ tables)
  'HISTORY'       --> Data from persisted history information (HOST_ tables)

- AGGREGATE_BY

  Aggregation criteria (possible values can be found in comment)

  'CALLSTACK'     --> Aggregation by callstack
  'HOST, PORT'    --> Aggregation by host and port
  'NONE'          --> No aggregation

- TIME_AGGREGATE_BY

  Aggregation criteria (possible values can be found in comment)

  'HOUR'          --> Aggregation by hour
  'YYYY/WW'       --> Aggregation by calendar week
  'TS<seconds>'   --> Time slice aggregation based on <seconds> seconds
  'NONE'          --> No aggregation

- ORDER_BY

  Sort criteria (available values are provided in comment)

  'TIME'          --> Sorting by time
  'COUNT'         --> Sorting by number of call stacks

[OUTPUT PARAMETERS]

- COUNT:            Number of threads (1 if no aggregation is done)
- PERCENT:          Percentage of threads compared to overall number of threads
- COMP:             Call stack components (see [INPUT_PARAMETERS] -> COMPONENTS for more details)
- THREAD_TYPE:      Thread type
- THREAD_CONTEXT:   Thread context (determined dynamically based on call stack)
- THREAD_ACTIVITY:  Thread activity (determined dynamically based on call stack)
- THREAD_STATE:     Thread state
- SAMPLE_TIME:      Sample time
- ST:               System replication site ID
- HOST:             Host name
- PORT:             Port
- THREAD_ID:        Thread ID
- CALL_<n>:         Call information for level <n>

[EXAMPLE OUTPUT]

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
|THREAD_TYPE  |THREAD_STATE            |THREADS|PERCENT|CALL_1                                                        |CALL_2                                                                                                  |CALL_3                                                                                                  |CALL_4                                                                                                 |
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
|SqlExecutor  |Running                 |     34|  49.27|UnifiedTable::DictionaryStorage::TemporaryValueBuffer::reserve|ltt::vector<int>::insertOverflow_                                                                       |AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdValuesBase<AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdBlockValues>::searchDocuments|AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdAttribute<AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdBlockValues>::searchDocuments|
|SqlExecutor  |Running                 |     20|  28.98|ltt::vector<int>::push_back                                   |AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdValuesBase<AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdBlockValues>::searchDocuments|AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdAttribute<AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdBlockValues>::searchDocuments |AttributeEngine::AttributeApi::searchDocuments                                                         |
|SqlExecutor  |Running                 |      5|   7.24|AttributeEngine::idattribute::BlockHandle::uncompress         |AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdBlockValuesIterator::readNext                                           |AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdValuesBase<AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdBlockValues>::searchDocuments|AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdAttribute<AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdBlockValues>::searchDocuments|
|SqlExecutor  |Running                 |      3|   4.34|AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdBlockValuesIterator::readNext |AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdValuesBase<AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdBlockValues>::searchDocuments|AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdAttribute<AttributeEngine::idattribute::IdBlockValues>::searchDocuments |AttributeEngine::AttributeApi::searchDocuments                                                         |
|Request      |Running                 |      2|   2.89|syscall+0x15                                                  |Synchronization::Semaphore::timedWait                                                                   |TrexThreads::PoolThread::run                                                                            |TrexThreads::PoolThread::run                                                                           |
|SqlExecutor  |Semaphore Wait          |      1|   1.44|syscall+0x15                                                  |Synchronization::BinarySemaphore::timedWait                                                             |TrexSync::Event::waitFor                                                                                |TrexThreads::Thread::join                                                                              |
|SqlExecutor  |ConditionalVariable Wait|      1|   1.44|syscall+0x15                                                  |Synchronization::CondVariable::timedWait                                                                |ptime::Transaction::tryToDelegateThrAndTimedWait                                                        |TrexStore::SyncQueue::wait                                                                             |
|RemoteService|Network Read            |      1|   1.44|syscall+0x15                                                  |Synchronization::Semaphore::timedWait                                                                   |TrexThreads::PoolThread::run                                                                            |TrexThreads::PoolThread::run                                                                           |
|SqlExecutor  |Running                 |      1|   1.44|void ltt::impl::introsortLoopAux<int*, long, ltt::less<int> > |void ltt::impl::introsortLoopAux<int*, long, ltt::less<int> >                                           |void ltt::impl::introsortLoopAux<int*, long, ltt::less<int> >                                           |void ltt::impl::introsortLoopAux<int*, long, ltt::less<int> >                                          |
|SqlExecutor  |Running                 |      1|   1.44|void ltt::impl::introsortLoopAux<int*, long, ltt::less<int> > |void ltt::impl::introsortLoopAux<int*, long, ltt::less<int> >                                           |void ltt::impl::introsortLoopAux<int*, long, ltt::less<int> >                                           |void ltt::sort<int*, ltt::less<int> >                                                                  |
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*/

BASIS_INFO AS
( SELECT
    CASE
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME =    'C'                             THEN CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME LIKE 'C-S%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, -SUBSTR_AFTER(BEGIN_TIME, 'C-S'))
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME LIKE 'C-M%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, -SUBSTR_AFTER(BEGIN_TIME, 'C-M') * 60)
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME LIKE 'C-H%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, -SUBSTR_AFTER(BEGIN_TIME, 'C-H') * 3600)
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME LIKE 'C-D%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, -SUBSTR_AFTER(BEGIN_TIME, 'C-D') * 86400)
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME LIKE 'C-W%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, -SUBSTR_AFTER(BEGIN_TIME, 'C-W') * 86400 * 7)
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME LIKE 'E-S%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP(END_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), -SUBSTR_AFTER(BEGIN_TIME, 'E-S'))
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME LIKE 'E-M%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP(END_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), -SUBSTR_AFTER(BEGIN_TIME, 'E-M') * 60)
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME LIKE 'E-H%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP(END_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), -SUBSTR_AFTER(BEGIN_TIME, 'E-H') * 3600)
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME LIKE 'E-D%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP(END_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), -SUBSTR_AFTER(BEGIN_TIME, 'E-D') * 86400)
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME LIKE 'E-W%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP(END_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), -SUBSTR_AFTER(BEGIN_TIME, 'E-W') * 86400 * 7)
      WHEN BEGIN_TIME =    'MIN'                           THEN TO_TIMESTAMP('1000/01/01 00:00:00', 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS')
      WHEN SUBSTR(BEGIN_TIME, 1, 1) NOT IN ('C', 'E', 'M') THEN TO_TIMESTAMP(BEGIN_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS')
    END BEGIN_TIME,
    CASE
      WHEN END_TIME =    'C'                             THEN CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
      WHEN END_TIME LIKE 'C-S%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, -SUBSTR_AFTER(END_TIME, 'C-S'))
      WHEN END_TIME LIKE 'C-M%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, -SUBSTR_AFTER(END_TIME, 'C-M') * 60)
      WHEN END_TIME LIKE 'C-H%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, -SUBSTR_AFTER(END_TIME, 'C-H') * 3600)
      WHEN END_TIME LIKE 'C-D%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, -SUBSTR_AFTER(END_TIME, 'C-D') * 86400)
      WHEN END_TIME LIKE 'C-W%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, -SUBSTR_AFTER(END_TIME, 'C-W') * 86400 * 7)
      WHEN END_TIME LIKE 'B+S%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP(BEGIN_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), SUBSTR_AFTER(END_TIME, 'B+S'))
      WHEN END_TIME LIKE 'B+M%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP(BEGIN_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), SUBSTR_AFTER(END_TIME, 'B+M') * 60)
      WHEN END_TIME LIKE 'B+H%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP(BEGIN_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), SUBSTR_AFTER(END_TIME, 'B+H') * 3600)
      WHEN END_TIME LIKE 'B+D%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP(BEGIN_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), SUBSTR_AFTER(END_TIME, 'B+D') * 86400)
      WHEN END_TIME LIKE 'B+W%'                          THEN ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP(BEGIN_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), SUBSTR_AFTER(END_TIME, 'B+W') * 86400 * 7)
      WHEN END_TIME =    'MAX'                           THEN TO_TIMESTAMP('9999/12/31 00:00:00', 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS')
      WHEN SUBSTR(END_TIME, 1, 1) NOT IN ('C', 'B', 'M') THEN TO_TIMESTAMP(END_TIME, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS')
    END END_TIME,
    TIMEZONE,
    SITE_ID,
    HOST,
    PORT,
    THREAD_ID,
    COMPONENTS,
    THREAD_TYPE,
    THREAD_CONTEXT,
    THREAD_ACTIVITY,
    THREAD_STATE,
    CALLSTACK_PATTERN,
    MAX_FRAME_LEVEL,
    MAX_CALL_LEN,
    ONLY_ACTIVE_THREADS,
    IGNORE_OWN_THREADS,
    ONLY_INDEX_HANDLE_CALLSTACKS,
    SHORT_CALLS,
    DATA_SOURCE,
    AGGREGATE_BY,
    MAP(TIME_AGGREGATE_BY,
      'NONE',        'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS',
      'HOUR',        'YYYY/MM/DD HH24',
      'DAY',         'YYYY/MM/DD (DY)',
      'HOUR_OF_DAY', 'HH24',
      TIME_AGGREGATE_BY ) TIME_AGGREGATE_BY,
    ORDER_BY
  FROM
  ( SELECT                     /* Modification section */
      'C-D1' BEGIN_TIME,                  /* YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS timestamp, C, C-S<seconds>, C-M<minutes>, C-H<hours>, C-D<days>, C-W<weeks>, E-S<seconds>, E-M<minutes>, E-H<hours>, E-D<days>, E-W<weeks>, MIN */
      'C' END_TIME,                    /* YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS timestamp, C, C-S<seconds>, C-M<minutes>, C-H<hours>, C-D<days>, C-W<weeks>, B+S<seconds>, B+M<minutes>, B+H<hours>, B+D<days>, B+W<weeks>, MAX */
      'SERVER' TIMEZONE,                              /* SERVER, UTC */
      -1 SITE_ID,
      '%' HOST,
      '%' PORT,
      -1 THREAD_ID,
      '%' COMPONENTS,
      '%' THREAD_TYPE,
      '%' THREAD_CONTEXT,
      '%' THREAD_ACTIVITY,
      '%' THREAD_STATE,
      '%' CALLSTACK_PATTERN,
      -1 MAX_FRAME_LEVEL,
      -1 MAX_CALL_LEN,
      'X' ONLY_ACTIVE_THREADS,
      'X' IGNORE_OWN_THREADS,
      ' ' ONLY_INDEX_HANDLE_CALLSTACKS,
      'X' SHORT_CALLS,
      'HISTORY' DATA_SOURCE,           /* CURRENT, HISTORY */
      'COMPONENTS, THREAD_TYPE, THREAD_CONTEXT, THREAD_ACTIVITY, THREAD_STATE, CALLSTACK' AGGREGATE_BY,     /* TIME, HOST, PORT, THREAD_ID, COMPONENTS, THREAD_TYPE, THREAD_CONTEXT, THREAD_ACTIVITY, THREAD_STATE, CALLSTACK or comma separated combinations, NONE for no aggregation */
      'NONE' TIME_AGGREGATE_BY,     /* HOUR, DAY, HOUR_OF_DAY or database time pattern, TS<seconds> for time slice, NONE for no aggregation */
      'COUNT' ORDER_BY               /* COUNT, TIME, STACK */
    FROM
      DUMMY
  )
),
CALLSTACKS AS
( SELECT
    *,
    CALL_1 || CALL_2 || CALL_3 || CALL_4 || CALL_5 || CALL_6 || CALL_7 || CALL_8 || CALL_9 || CALL_10 ||
    CALL_11 || CALL_12 || CALL_13 || CALL_14 || CALL_15 || CALL_16 || CALL_17 || CALL_18 || CALL_19 || CALL_20 ||
    CALL_21 || CALL_22 || CALL_23 || CALL_24 || CALL_25 || CALL_26 || CALL_27 || CALL_28 || CALL_29 || CALL_30 ||
    CALL_31 || CALL_32 || CALL_33 || CALL_34 || CALL_35 || CALL_36 || CALL_37 || CALL_38 || CALL_39 || CALL_40 ||
    CALL_41 || CALL_42 || CALL_43 || CALL_44 || CALL_45 || CALL_46 || CALL_47 || CALL_48 || CALL_49 || CALL_50 ||
    CALL_51 || CALL_52 || CALL_53 || CALL_54 || CALL_55 || CALL_56 || CALL_57 || CALL_58 || CALL_59 || CALL_60 ||
    CALL_61 || CALL_62 || CALL_63 || CALL_64 || CALL_65 || CALL_66 || CALL_67 || CALL_68 || CALL_69 || CALL_70 ||
    CALL_71 || CALL_72 || CALL_73 || CALL_74 || CALL_75 || CALL_76 || CALL_77 || CALL_78 || CALL_79 || CALL_80 ||
    CALL_81 || CALL_82 || CALL_83 || CALL_84 || CALL_85 || CALL_86 || CALL_87 || CALL_88 || CALL_89 || CALL_90 CALLSTACK_CONCAT
  FROM
  ( SELECT
      C.SAMPLE_TIME,
      C.SITE_ID,
      C.HOST,
      C.PORT,
      C.THREAD_ID,
      C.IS_ACTIVE,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL,  1, C.FRAME_NAME, '')) CALL_1_ORIGINAL,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL,  1, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_1,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL,  2, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_2,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL,  3, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_3,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL,  4, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_4,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL,  5, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_5,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL,  6, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_6,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL,  7, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_7,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL,  8, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_8,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL,  9, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_9,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 10, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_10,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 11, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_11,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 12, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_12,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 13, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_13,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 14, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_14,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 15, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_15,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 16, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_16,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 17, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_17,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 18, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_18,  
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 19, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_19,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 20, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_20,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 21, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_21,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 22, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_22,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 23, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_23,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 24, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_24,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 25, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_25,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 26, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_26,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 27, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_27,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 28, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_28,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 29, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_29,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 30, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_30,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 31, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_31,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 32, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_32,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 33, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_33,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 34, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_34,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 35, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_35,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 36, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_36,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 37, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_37,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 38, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_38,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 39, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_39,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 40, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_40,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 41, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_41,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 42, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_42,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 43, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_43,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 44, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_44,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 45, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_45,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 46, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_46,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 47, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_47,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 48, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_48,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 49, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_49,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 50, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_50,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 51, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_51,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 52, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_52,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 53, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_53,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 54, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_54,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 55, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_55,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 56, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_56,

      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 77, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_77,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 78, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_78,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 79, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_79,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 80, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_80,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 81, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_81,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 82, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_82,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 83, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_83,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 84, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_84,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 85, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_85,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 86, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_86,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 87, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_87,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 88, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_88,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 89, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_89,
      MAX(MAP(C.FRAME_LEVEL, 90, MAP(BI.SHORT_CALLS, 'X', C.FRAME_SHORT, C.FRAME_NAME), '')) CALL_90
    FROM
      BASIS_INFO BI,
    ( SELECT
        SAMPLE_TIME,
        SITE_ID,
        HOST,
        PORT,
        THREAD_ID,
        IS_ACTIVE,
        FRAME_LEVEL,
        SUBSTR(F, 1, LEAST(MAP(INSTR(F, '('), 0, 999, INSTR(F, '(')), MAP(INSTR(F, '+0x'), 0, 999, INSTR(F, '+0x'))) - 1) FRAME_SHORT,
        FRAME_NAME
      FROM
      ( SELECT
          CURRENT_TIMESTAMP SAMPLE_TIME,
          CURRENT_SITE_ID() SITE_ID,
          C.HOST,
          C.PORT,
          C.THREAD_ID,
          C.IS_ACTIVE,
          C.FRAME_LEVEL,
          REPLACE(REPLACE(C.FRAME_NAME, '(anonymous namespace)::', ''), '> >', '>') F,
          C.FRAME_NAME
        FROM
          BASIS_INFO BI,
          M_SERVICE_THREAD_CALLSTACKS C
        WHERE
          BI.DATA_SOURCE = 'CURRENT' AND
          ( BI.SITE_ID = -1 OR ( BI.SITE_ID = 0 AND CURRENT_SITE_ID() IN (-1, 0) ) OR CURRENT_SITE_ID() = BI.SITE_ID ) AND
          C.HOST LIKE BI.HOST AND
          TO_VARCHAR(C.PORT) LIKE BI.PORT AND
          ( BI.THREAD_ID = -1 OR C.THREAD_ID = BI.THREAD_ID ) AND
          ( BI.MAX_FRAME_LEVEL = -1 OR C.FRAME_LEVEL <= BI.MAX_FRAME_LEVEL )
        UNION ALL
        SELECT
          C.SERVER_TIMESTAMP SAMPLE_TIME,
          C.SITE_ID,
          C.HOST,
          C.PORT,
          C.THREAD_ID,
          C.IS_ACTIVE,
          C.FRAME_LEVEL,
          REPLACE(REPLACE(C.FRAME_NAME, '(anonymous namespace)::', ''), '> >', '>') F,
          C.FRAME_NAME
        FROM
          BASIS_INFO BI,
          _SYS_STATISTICS.HOST_SERVICE_THREAD_CALLSTACKS C
        WHERE
          BI.DATA_SOURCE = 'HISTORY' AND
          ( BI.SITE_ID = -1 OR ( BI.SITE_ID = 0 AND C.SITE_ID IN (-1, 0) ) OR C.SITE_ID = BI.SITE_ID ) AND
          C.HOST LIKE BI.HOST AND
          TO_VARCHAR(C.PORT) LIKE BI.PORT AND
          CASE BI.TIMEZONE WHEN 'UTC' THEN ADD_SECONDS(C.SERVER_TIMESTAMP, SECONDS_BETWEEN(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, CURRENT_UTCTIMESTAMP)) ELSE C.SERVER_TIMESTAMP END BETWEEN BI.BEGIN_TIME AND BI.END_TIME AND
          ( BI.THREAD_ID = -1 OR C.THREAD_ID = BI.THREAD_ID ) AND
          ( BI.MAX_FRAME_LEVEL = -1 OR C.FRAME_LEVEL <= BI.MAX_FRAME_LEVEL )
      )
    ) C
    GROUP BY
      C.SAMPLE_TIME,
      C.SITE_ID,
      C.HOST,
      C.PORT,
      C.THREAD_ID,
      C.IS_ACTIVE
  )
),
INDEX_HANDLE_METHODS AS
( SELECT '%CS::OC::OptimizeCompressionHelper::changeCompression%' METHOD FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%CS::OC::OptimizeCompressionHelper::commitRowOrder%' FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%Executor::PlanExecutor::doCalculateSingleThreaded%' FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%hex::planex::ExecutablePlan::open%' FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%ItabCreateGuard::~ItabCreateGuard%' FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%JoinEvaluator::TableAccess::jeReadIndex%' FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%*::mgetSearch%' FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%ptime::MixedJoin_inverted_index::do_fetch%' FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%qo3::OptimizerImpl::evaluate%' FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%TRexAPI::PartSearchImpl::doSearch%' FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%TRexAPI::SearchAPI::materializeItab%' FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%TRexUtils::Parallel::Sorter%' FROM DUMMY UNION ALL
  SELECT '%bwMergeDictGetValueIdFn%' FROM DUMMY
)

      CALL_75,
      CALL_76,
      CALL_77,
      CALL_78,
      CALL_79,
      CALL_80,
      CALL_81,
      CALL_82,
      CALL_83,
      CALL_84,
      CALL_85,
      CALL_86,
      CALL_87,
      CALL_88,
      CALL_89,
      CALL_90,
      ORDER_BY
    FROM
    ( SELECT
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'TIME')          != 0
          THEN
            CASE
              WHEN BI.TIME_AGGREGATE_BY LIKE 'TS%' THEN
                TO_VARCHAR(ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP('2014/01/01 00:00:00', 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), FLOOR(SECONDS_BETWEEN(TO_TIMESTAMP('2014/01/01 00:00:00',
                'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), CASE BI.TIMEZONE WHEN 'UTC' THEN ADD_SECONDS(TC.SAMPLE_TIME, SECONDS_BETWEEN(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, CURRENT_UTCTIMESTAMP)) ELSE TC.SAMPLE_TIME END) / SUBSTR(BI.TIME_AGGREGATE_BY, 3)) * SUBSTR(BI.TIME_AGGREGATE_BY, 3)), 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS')
              ELSE TO_VARCHAR(CASE BI.TIMEZONE WHEN 'UTC' THEN ADD_SECONDS(TC.SAMPLE_TIME, SECONDS_BETWEEN(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, CURRENT_UTCTIMESTAMP)) ELSE TC.SAMPLE_TIME END, BI.TIME_AGGREGATE_BY)
            END
          ELSE 'any'
        END SAMPLE_TIME,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'SITE_ID')         != 0 THEN TO_VARCHAR(TC.SITE_ID)         ELSE MAP(BI.SITE_ID, -1, 'any', TO_VARCHAR(BI.SITE_ID))            END SITE_ID,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'HOST')            != 0 THEN TC.HOST                        ELSE MAP(BI.HOST,            '%', 'any', BI.HOST)                  END HOST,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'PORT')            != 0 THEN TO_VARCHAR(TC.PORT)            ELSE MAP(BI.PORT,            '%', 'any', BI.PORT)                  END PORT,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'THREAD_ID')       != 0 THEN TO_VARCHAR(TC.THREAD_ID)       ELSE MAP(BI.THREAD_ID,       -1,  'any', TO_VARCHAR(BI.THREAD_ID)) END THREAD_ID,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'COMPONENTS')      != 0 THEN TC.COMPONENTS                  ELSE MAP(BI.COMPONENTS,      '%', 'any', BI.COMPONENTS)            END COMPONENTS,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'THREAD_TYPE')     != 0 THEN TC.THREAD_TYPE                 ELSE MAP(BI.THREAD_TYPE,     '%', 'any', BI.THREAD_TYPE)           END THREAD_TYPE,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'THREAD_CONTEXT')  != 0 THEN TC.THREAD_CONTEXT              ELSE MAP(BI.THREAD_CONTEXT,  '%', 'any', BI.THREAD_CONTEXT)        END THREAD_CONTEXT,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'THREAD_ACTIVITY') != 0 THEN TC.THREAD_ACTIVITY             ELSE MAP(BI.THREAD_ACTIVITY, '%', 'any', BI.THREAD_ACTIVITY)       END THREAD_ACTIVITY,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'THREAD_STATE')    != 0 THEN TC.THREAD_STATE                ELSE MAP(BI.THREAD_STATE,    '%', 'any', BI.THREAD_STATE)          END THREAD_STATE,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_1,  SUBSTR(TC.CALL_1,  1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_1,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_2,  SUBSTR(TC.CALL_2,  1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_2,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_3,  SUBSTR(TC.CALL_3,  1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_3,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_4,  SUBSTR(TC.CALL_4,  1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_4,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_5,  SUBSTR(TC.CALL_5,  1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_5,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_6,  SUBSTR(TC.CALL_6,  1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_6,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_7,  SUBSTR(TC.CALL_7,  1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_7,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_8,  SUBSTR(TC.CALL_8,  1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_8,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_9,  SUBSTR(TC.CALL_9,  1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_9,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_10, SUBSTR(TC.CALL_10, 1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_10,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_11, SUBSTR(TC.CALL_11, 1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_11,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_12, SUBSTR(TC.CALL_12, 1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_12,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_13, SUBSTR(TC.CALL_13, 1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_13,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_14, SUBSTR(TC.CALL_14, 1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_14,

        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'CALLSTACK')     != 0 THEN MAP(BI.MAX_CALL_LEN, -1, TC.CALL_90, SUBSTR(TC.CALL_90, 1, BI.MAX_CALL_LEN)) ELSE 'any' END CALL_90,
        COUNT(*) THREADS,
        COUNT(*) / SUM(COUNT(*)) OVER () * 100 PERCENT,
        BI.SHORT_CALLS,
        BI.ORDER_BY,
        TC.CALLSTACK_CONCAT
      FROM
        BASIS_INFO BI,
      ( SELECT
          *,
          CASE   WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%AttributeEngine::%'               THEN 'A' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%TrexCalculationEngine::%'         THEN 'C' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%ESX::%'                           THEN 'E' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%federation::%'                    THEN 'F' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%hex::%'                           THEN 'H' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%::JE%' OR
                      CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%JoinEvaluator::%'                 THEN 'J' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%ljit%' OR
                      CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%Llang%'                           THEN 'L' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%ptime::LVCProcedure::execute%' OR
                      CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%liveCache%' OR
                      LOCATE (CALLSTACK_CONCAT, 'LVC_') > 0                     THEN 'Li' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'memcpy%' OR
                      CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%MemoryManager::%' OR
                      CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'memset%'                           THEN 'M' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '__libc_recv%' OR
                      CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '__libc_send%' OR
                      CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '__libc_write%' OR
                      CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%TrexNet::%'                       THEN 'N' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%OlapEngine::%'                    THEN 'O' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN ( CALL_1_ORIGINAL LIKE '%ld-linux-x86-64.so%' OR
                        CALL_1_ORIGINAL LIKE '%libc.so%' OR
                        CALL_1_ORIGINAL LIKE '%libm.so%' OR
                        CALL_1_ORIGINAL LIKE '%libpthread.so%' OR
                        CALL_1_ORIGINAL LIKE '%libstdc++.so%' OR
                        CALL_1_ORIGINAL LIKE '%[vdso]%' OR
                        SUBSTR(CALL_1_ORIGINAL, 1, 7) = '__GI___'
                      ) AND
                      CALL_1_ORIGINAL NOT LIKE 'syscall%' AND
                      CALL_1_ORIGINAL NOT LIKE '__libc_poll%'                   THEN 'Os' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%PlanningEngine::%'                THEN 'P' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%qo3::%'                           THEN 'Q' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%ptime::%' OR
                      CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%RowEngine::%'                     THEN 'R' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%sqlscript::%'                     THEN 'S' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%SQL::Update%'                     THEN 'U' ELSE '' END ||
            CASE WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%Executor::X2%'                    THEN 'X' ELSE '' END
            COMPONENTS,
          CASE
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%Execution::impl::NativeContextImpl::run%'                       THEN '3rd party Thread'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%TRexAPI::PostAssignThread::run%'                                THEN 'Assign'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%Distribution::DMLLogQueueProcessorThread::run%'                 THEN 'AsyncReplicationDMLLogReplayer'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%Backup::BackupExe_LogWaitForBackintConnectionThread::run%'      THEN 'BackupExe_LogWaitForBackintConnectionThread'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%Backup::Channel::PipelineFilter::run%'                          THEN 'BackupPipelineFilter'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%BufferCacheManager::BufferCacheHKThread::run%'                  THEN 'BufferCacheHKThread'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%TrexCalculationEngine::ManagerGarbageCollectionThread::run%'    THEN 'CalcEngineGarbageCollector'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%ptime::CallstackThread::run%'                                   THEN 'Callstack'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%FileAccess::LocalFileCompletionThread::run%'                    THEN 'CompletionThread'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%DataAccess::ContinuousPageFlusher::run%'                        THEN 'ContinuousPageFlusher'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%StatisticsService::NameServerControllerThread::run%'            THEN 'ControllerThread (StatisticsServer)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%NameServer::DirSizeJob::run%'                                   THEN 'DirSize'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%DPDistributor::DistributorExecutor::run%'                       THEN 'DPDistributor'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%DPReceiver::PersistentTranDataCleaner::run%'                    THEN 'DPReceiverCleaner'

            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'Synchronization::NonrecursiveMutex::updateStatistics%'                        THEN 'Synchronization (NonrecursiveMutex updateStatistics)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'Synchronization::ReadWriteLock::lockExclusive%'                               THEN 'Synchronization (ReadWriteLock lockExclusive)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'Synchronization::ReadWriteLock::setSharedOwner%'                              THEN 'Synchronization (ReadWriteLock setSharedOwner)'

            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'Synchronization::ReadWriteLock::unlockExclusive%'                             THEN 'Synchronization (ReadWriteLock unlockExclusive)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'Synchronization::ReadWriteLock::unlockSharedLL%'                              THEN 'Synchronization (ReadWriteLock unlockSharedLL)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'Synchronization::Semaphore::signal%'                                          THEN 'Synchronization (Semaphore signal)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'Synchronization::Semaphore::timedWait%'                                       THEN 'Synchronization (Semaphore timedWait)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'Synchronization::SpeculativeLock%::begin%'                                    THEN 'Synchronization (SpeculativeLock begin)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%Synchronization::SynchronizationPrimitiveBase::setSyncWaiting%'              THEN 'Synchronization (SynchronizationPrimitiveBase setSyncWaiting)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'Synchronization::SystemMutexBase::unlock%'                                    THEN 'Synchronization (SystemMutexBase unlock)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'Synchronization::tpause%'                                                     THEN 'Synchronization (tpause)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%Synchronization::TSXStatisticsHandler%::tx_stats_update%'                    THEN 'Synchronization (TSXStatisticsHandler tx_stats_update)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'TRexAPI::JoinSearchImpl::executeSearch%'                                      THEN 'TRexAPI (JoinSearchImpl executeSearch)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%TRexAPI::PartSearchImpl::doSearch%'                                          THEN 'TRexAPI (PartSearchImpl doSearch)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'TRexAPI::TRexApiSearch::search%'                                              THEN 'TRexAPI (TRexApiSearch search)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%TRexCommonObjects::DefaultColumnDict%'                                       THEN 'TRexCommonObjects (DefaultColumnDict)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%TrexNet::Ext::WorkerThread::runImpl%'                                        THEN 'TrexNet (Ext WorkerThread runImpl)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%TrexNet::NetInput::peek_nb%'                                                 THEN 'TrexNet (netInput peek_nb)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%TRexUtils::Parallel::Context::wait%'                                         THEN 'TRexUtils (Parallel Context wait)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%TRexUtils::WildcardPattern%::matchInternal2%'                                THEN 'TRexUtils (WildcardPattern matchInternal2)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%tx::TimestampTracker::updateMinTimestamp%'                                   THEN 'tx (TimestampTracker updateMinTimestamp)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%WorkerThread.cpp%'                                                           THEN 'WorkerThread.cpp'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'xtoa%'                                                                        THEN 'xtoa'

            ELSE ''
          END THREAD_ACTIVITY,
          CASE
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%Synchronization::Barrier::wait%'                                             THEN 'Barrier Wait'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%__clock_nanosleep%'                                                          THEN 'Sleeping'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%Execution::sleep%'                                                           THEN 'Sleeping'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '%__GI___nanosleep%'                                                           THEN 'Sleeping'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'ptime::Futex::lock%'                                                          THEN 'ptime (Futex lock)'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'syscall%Synchronization::CondVariable::timedWait%'                            THEN 'ConditionalVariable Wait'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'syscall%Synchronization::CondVariable::wait%'                                 THEN 'ConditionalVariable Wait'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'syscall%Synchronization::ReadWriteLock::timedWaitLockExclusive%'              THEN 'ExclusiveLock Enter'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'syscall%Execution::JobBarrier::wait%'                                         THEN 'Job Exec Waiting'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '__pthread_mutex_lock%'                                                        THEN 'Mutex Wait'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '__pthread_mutex_timedlock%'                                                   THEN 'Mutex Wait'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'syscall%Synchronization::NonrecursiveMutex::lockInternal%'                    THEN 'Mutex Wait'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'syscall%Synchronization::Mutex::lockInternal%'                                THEN 'Mutex Wait'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '__GI___poll%'                                                                 THEN 'Network Poll'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE '__pthread_cond_wait%'                                                         THEN 'POSIX Thread Condition Wait'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'syscall%Synchronization::Semaphore::timedWait%'                               THEN 'Semaphore Wait'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'syscall%Synchronization::BinarySemaphore::timedWait%'                         THEN 'Semaphore Wait'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'syscall%Synchronization::ReadWriteLock::lockShared%'                          THEN 'SharedLock Enter'
            WHEN CALLSTACK_CONCAT LIKE 'syscall%Synchronization::ReadWriteLock::timedWaitLockSharedLL%'               THEN 'SharedLock Enter'
            ELSE 'Running'
          END THREAD_STATE
        FROM
          CALLSTACKS
      ) TC
      WHERE
        TC.HOST LIKE BI.HOST AND
        TO_VARCHAR(TC.PORT) LIKE BI.PORT AND
        ( BI.THREAD_ID = -1 OR BI.THREAD_ID = TC.THREAD_ID ) AND
        TC.COMPONENTS LIKE BI.COMPONENTS AND
        TC.THREAD_TYPE LIKE BI.THREAD_TYPE AND
        TC.THREAD_CONTEXT LIKE BI.THREAD_CONTEXT AND
        TC.THREAD_ACTIVITY LIKE BI.THREAD_ACTIVITY AND
        TC.THREAD_STATE LIKE BI.THREAD_STATE AND
        ( BI.ONLY_ACTIVE_THREADS = ' ' OR TC.IS_ACTIVE = 'TRUE' ) AND
        ( BI.IGNORE_OWN_THREADS = ' ' OR BI.DATA_SOURCE = 'HISTORY' OR NOT EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM M_SERVICE_THREADS ST WHERE ST.CONNECTION_ID = CURRENT_CONNECTION AND ST.HOST = TC.HOST AND ST.THREAD_ID = TC.THREAD_ID) ) AND
        UPPER(TC.CALLSTACK_CONCAT) LIKE UPPER(BI.CALLSTACK_PATTERN)
      GROUP BY
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'TIME')          != 0
          THEN
            CASE
              WHEN BI.TIME_AGGREGATE_BY LIKE 'TS%' THEN
                TO_VARCHAR(ADD_SECONDS(TO_TIMESTAMP('2014/01/01 00:00:00', 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), FLOOR(SECONDS_BETWEEN(TO_TIMESTAMP('2014/01/01 00:00:00',
                'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS'), CASE BI.TIMEZONE WHEN 'UTC' THEN ADD_SECONDS(TC.SAMPLE_TIME, SECONDS_BETWEEN(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, CURRENT_UTCTIMESTAMP)) ELSE TC.SAMPLE_TIME END) / SUBSTR(BI.TIME_AGGREGATE_BY, 3)) * SUBSTR(BI.TIME_AGGREGATE_BY, 3)), 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS')
              ELSE TO_VARCHAR(CASE BI.TIMEZONE WHEN 'UTC' THEN ADD_SECONDS(TC.SAMPLE_TIME, SECONDS_BETWEEN(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, CURRENT_UTCTIMESTAMP)) ELSE TC.SAMPLE_TIME END, BI.TIME_AGGREGATE_BY)
            END
          ELSE 'any'
        END,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'SITE_ID')         != 0 THEN TO_VARCHAR(TC.SITE_ID)         ELSE MAP(BI.SITE_ID, -1, 'any', TO_VARCHAR(BI.SITE_ID))            END,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'HOST')            != 0 THEN TC.HOST                        ELSE MAP(BI.HOST,            '%', 'any', BI.HOST)                  END,
        CASE WHEN BI.AGGREGATE_BY = 'NONE' OR INSTR(BI.AGGREGATE_BY, 'PORT')            != 0 THEN TO_VARCHAR(TC.PORT)            ELSE MAP(BI.PORT,            '%', 'any', BI.PORT)                  END,
